Subject: [dm-l] Workshop and Aliento 6th International Conference Nancy-Paris,

Dear Colleagues,

We are happy to announce the 6th Aliento International Conference which 
will be held at Nancy and Paris on March 15-17, 2016. 
(http://www.aliento.eu)

Please find hereby the call for papers for the Workshop dedicated to 
Digital Humanities (Nancy, March 16)

Hoping you will be able to participate, we send our best regards,

Marie-Christine Bornes Varol

Professeur des Universités (Inalco)
